Basel O
II O
Application O
, O
Basel O
II O
is O
the O

, O
which O
are O

on O

and O

issued O
by O

Basel O
Committee O
on O

. O
The O

Basel O
II O
, O
which O
was O

published O
in O
June O
2004 O
, O
is O
to O

an O

standard O
that O

regulators O
can O
use O
when O
creating O
regulations O
about O
how O
much O
capital O
banks O
need O
to O
put O
aside O
to O
guard O
against O
the O
types O
of O
financial O
and O
operational O
risks O
banks O
face O

. O
In O
practice O
, O

II O
attempts O
to O

this O
by O

up O

risk O
and O
capital O
management O
requirements O
designed O
to O
ensure O
that O
a O
bank O
holds O
capital O

appropriate O
to O
the O
risk O

bank O

through O

and O
investment O
practices O

. O
The O
New O
Accord O
includes O
several O
methodologies O
for O

a O

's O
risk O
- O
based O

requirements O
for O

, O

and O

risk O

. O
For O

Based O
Capital O
( O

) O
, O

( O

) O

Test O
( O
ST O
) O
, O

that O
will O

for O

Simple O
VaR O

. O

. O
